 Political Background The 1951 and 1957 elections were won by PC Bose of Congress from Dhanbad Lok Sabha seat
 1962 main is seat se congress piaar chakravarti jeetne main kaamyaab hue
 Independent candidate Rani Lalitha won Rajya Lakshmi in 1967
 1971 main phir is seat par congress ne vaapasi kii or uske tikat par ram narayan sharma jite
 In 1977, this seat was captured by the Communist Party and its ticket was won by AK Roy
 1980 ke chunaav main bhi eke roy jeetne main kaamyaab hue
 In 1984, Congress returned and won on its ticket Shankar Dayal Singh
 1989 kaa chunaav communist party ke hi eke roy jite or teesri baar saansad bane
 In 1991, the bjp's account opened on this seat for the first time and Rita Verma won on her ticket
 vah lagaataar chaar baar (1991, 1996, 1998 or 1999) jeetin
 She was also a minister of several ministries in the Atal Bihari government
 2004 main is seat se congress ke chandra shekhar doobe jite
 In 2009, the BJP returned and won Pashupati Nath Singh on its ticket
 2014 main vah apni seat bachaane main kaamyaab hue
 The social Tanabanadhanabad Lok Sabha seat is dominated by urban voters
 is seat par kareeb 62 fisadi shahari matadaata or 38 fisadi gramin matadaata he

 iske alaava seat par uttar pradesh, bihar or pashchim bengal ke logon kii acchhee taadaat he

 Know those 10 things, Raghuram Rajan said that for the Indian economy, these cannot be ignored: 1
 raghuram rajan ne kendra sarkaar ke saamne avastavik apekshaaon kii ore ishaara kiya
 For this, he also used the phrase 'ronald Reagan sitting on a white horse'
 isapar kehete hue rajan ne kaha ki desh main aarthik vruddhi kii jimmedaari sarkaar kii hoti he kyonki nijee or sarkari kshetra ke saath milakar nivesh kaa kaam unhen hi karnaa hota he
 2
 rajan ne kaha ki rigerv bank kaa kaam rupye ke mulya, mahangaai dar or vyapak aarthik sthirataa ko dekhte hue vishwaas kaa maahaul kaayam karnaa rahata he
 With this, the central bank helps the government in some structural reforms, so by the end of August, licenses will be given to small financial banks to speed up business in the country
 3
 The head of the central bank believes that the country's economy has inherited many problems and as we solve those problems, the country's economic growth will accelerate
 lihaaja, desh main ataki hui kuch ahm pariyojnaon ke liye rasta taiyaar karne kii jarurat he
 4
 rajan ne kaha ki desh main pehle manmarjee se nitiyaan banaai jaati thi
 The brunt of this is that the entire economy has to suffer for a long time
 lihaaja, jaise jaise desh tarakkee ke raste par jayega vaastavik apekshaaon kaa nirmaan karne vaali sansthaaen bhi viksit hongi
 5
 monsoon kamjor rahane se arthvyavastha ke liye dikkatein ko badhengi lekin usase ahm baat yah he ki monsoon kamjor rahane par sarkaar kii pratikriya kya rahati he
 If the government has the appropriate policy solutions to deal with a bad monsoon, then the losses from it can be avoided
 6
 Crude oil prices make a big difference in the Indian economy
 jis tarah se pichley saal keemton main giravat ai, sarkaar ko atirikt bajet se anya sansadhano ko urja dene main madad mili
 However, the increase in its prices in the last few days is a problem
 kendriya bank ko ummid he ki bazaar main ek baar phir kachche tel kii aapurti jarurat se zyada hogi or keemton main giravat se sarkaar ke bajet ko phayda milegaa
 7
 byaaj daron ko ghataane kaa laabh dhire-dhire upabhoktaaon tak pahunch rahaa he
 Other banks are also cutting their interest rates
 haalanki, rigerv bank kii najar byaaj daron ko sanchalit karne main bainko par hone vaale asar par he
 Rajan said that in order to make banks competitive in the country it is necessary to come on a day when all banks will be able to decide their rates on the basis of competition
 8
 This is a major economic reform
 rigerv bank ko ummid he ki janvari 2016 tak vah banking ke is sudhaar ko lagu kar sakenge
 Rajan said that by the end of the current financial year, all banks will be brought up to the marginal cost price
 9
 We have inherited land disputes in the country
 yah samasya bhi vikaas se paidaa hui he
 It is clear from the ongoing debate on land acquisition that the government has to create the necessary environment to take steps towards its priorities
 sarkaar ko adivaasiyon ke adhikaron ke saath-saath urja jaruraton ke liye mining bhi karnaa he
 Therefore, there is a need to create such a strategy so that there is no conflict
 10
 On the threat of foreign capital exit, Raghuram Rajan said that decisions in the US will have an impact on India
 haalanki shuruaati asthirataa ke vakt kuch niveshak apana paisa nikaal sakate hai lekin sthirataa waapas aane par niveshak uchit faisla lenge
 Therefore, our effort is to maintain basic strength and through that the growth of economic development in the country will be steady and fast

 At the end of June, the National Investigation Agency (NIA) arrested seven people from Hyderabad on charges of belonging to terrorist organization ISIS and plotting to attack India
 enditivi ko un 7 main se 5 logon ke bayaan mili hai, jo ki bharat main iesas kii pahunch ko lekar kai pareshaan karne vaale pahaluon ko ujagar karte hai
 These shows how this terrorist organization arranges arms and explosives for its operatives in at least 3 Indian states
 aropiyon dwaara hiraasat main die gaye bayaan court main subut ke taur par to istemaal nahin ho sakate, lekin enie kaa kahana he ki digital records, jabt hue hathiyaaron, gola barood or visphotakon ke saath-saath gavaahon ke bayanon se in ikbaalia bayanon kii pushti hoti he
 According to the NIA, the prime suspect of the plot is Abraham Yazdani, a 31-year-old engineer hailing from the old city of Hyderabad, who was first attracted to ISIS during his job in Saudi Arabia
 ibrahim ne 28 pannon ke apane vistrut bayaan main kaha he ki vah abu isa al amareeki naam ke ek online handler ke sampark main tha, jisane usase syria jane ko kaha tha
 However, despite many applications, he could not get a visa
 jiske baad handler ne use bharat main hi rukne or yahaan apane jaise kuch or logon kaa samooh banaakar hamale karne ko kaha

 Former India fast bowler Chetan Sharma, who was the hero of India's win over England in the 1986 Test series, has advised Team India
 ek agast se shuru hone vaali paanch test maichon kii siries se pehle unhone bhartiya tej gendbaajon ko short pich gend karne se bachane or ‘upar gend daalane’ (short of gudlength) ko kaha he
 Chetan laid the foundation for India's victory by taking five wickets for 64 runs in the first innings of the first Test match at Lord's in the 1986 round
 iske baad unhone birmingham main tisare test match main das wicket chatkaaye the
 India won the series 2–0
 bharat kii taraf se 23 test maichon main 61 wicket lene vaale sharma ne kaha ki 32 saal pehle upar gend daalane, use move or swing karaane kii ranneeti apanaai thi, jisase unhen safalataa mili
 He advised Ishant Sharma, Umesh Yadav and Mohammed Shami's Indian fast bowling trinity to adopt the same strategy
 sharma ne pitiai se kaha, ‘paristhitiyon par kaaphi kuch nirbhar karata he, lekin vahaan se jaisi khabaren aa rahi hai usase lagata he ki tej gendbaajon ke liye mausam bahut acha ho gaya he
 It is raining and there will be moisture on the wicket
 main hameshaa se kahata rahaa hum ki england main aap jitna upar gend daalenge, to gend adhik swing hogi
 There will be no benefit from bowling short pitches
 ’unhone kaha, ‘aaj kal ke jamaane main gati se or short pich gendon se koi darataa nahin he
 You have to put the ball up, move it
 agar aap short of gudlength main gend karaate hai, to vah swat: hi move karegi or wicket milenge
 Sharma believes that in the limited overs series, fast bowlers did not get the expected success due to short pitch balls

 nichle kram main david miller ne 21 gend par naabad 36 ran kii tufaani pari kheli jisase pehle ballebaaji kaa faisla karne vaala dakshin africa paanch wicket par 304 ran kaa vishaal score khadaa karne main safal rahaa
 Sri Lanka's team 40 in response
 3 over main 229 ran par out ho gai
 By the time Kumar Sangakkara (88) was at the crease, the match looked lively but it was not too late for South Africa to register a win as soon as they were out
 dakshin africa kii taraf se leg spinner imran taahir ne 50 ran dekar teen wicket liye jabaki del sten, morne morkal or reyaan maclaren ne do-do wicket hasil kiye
 Sri Lanka started well in front of a big goal
 kushal perera (34) or tillakaratne dilashaan (40) ne pehle wicket ke liye 50 ran jode
 Sangakkara played the anchor after landing at the crease and shared a 48-run partnership for the second wicket with Dilshan
 iske baad haalanki srilanka ne niyamit antaraal main wicket ganvaae jisase duusare chor par khadey sangakaara par dabaav badha
 Sangakkara was also under pressure due to a wicket falling from the other end and in such a situation, despite being close to a century, mclaren's ball was caught waving in the air
 maclaren ne isi over main pehle lahiru thirimane (15) ko out kiya tha
 Sangakkara played 84 balls in his innings and hit nine fours
 isse pehle dakshin africa kii pari amala ke ird gird gumti rahi jinhone quinton di cock (27) or kallis (shunya) ke out hone ke baad divilliars ke saath milakar team ko majboot score tak pahunchane main ahm bhoomika nibhaai
 The useful contributions of Miller and mclaren (22 not out) in the slog overs helped the team cross 300 runs
 srilanka kii taraf se spinner anjata mendis ne 61 ran dekar teen wicket liye
 The next match of the series of three odis between these two teams will be played on July 9 in Pallikal
 mahesh bhupati or mark noles ne french open ke purush yugal main yahaan sidhe seton main jeet darj karke apane abhiyaan kii shandaar shuruyaat kii
 Bhupathi and his Bahamas partner Knowles defeated the French pair of Joslin Oana and Jo Wilfed Tsonga 6-3 6-2
 bhupati or noles kii chauthi variyata praapt jodi kaa match par is kadar dabadabaa rahaa ki unhen kisi bhi samay brake point ganvaane ke dabaav se nahin guzarana padaa
 Both of them won in just 58 minutes
 duusare daur main unka muqabla sweden ke johaan bunstrom or holland ke jin julian roger kii jodi se hoga
 Japan's women's team defeated host India on Friday in their fourth round robin match of Hero FIH Hockey World League Round-2 at Major Dhyanchand National Stadium
 match kaa faisla penalty shoot out ke jariye hua
 By the time the two teams were tied 2–2
 is haar ke baavjood bhartiya team talika main sheersh par kaayam he
 According to the FIH rules set for this tournament, if a round-robin match is on par for the scheduled time, teams have to draw a result through a penalty shootout
 penalty shootout main jeetne vaali team ko vining dra (dra jeetne vaali) team kaha jaataa he jabaki haarane vaali team ko loojing dra (dra haarane vaali) team kaha jaataa he
 The winning team gets two points and the losing team gets one point
 is tarah is match se bharat ko ek ank praapt hua jabaki japan ne do ank hasil kiye
 Japan now has 10 points
 itane hi ank bharat ke bhi hai lekin isse pehle ke sabhi muqablon main japan se behatar pradarshan karne ke kaaran bharat chah tiimon kii talika main pehle sthaan par kaayam he
 Japan is in second place
 japan ne apni vipakshi tiimon ke khilaaf 25 gol kiye hai jabaki bharat ne 21 gol kiye hai
 India has won three matches while in one match it has been a losing draw team
 duusari ore, japan ne chaar me se do match jite hai jabaki do maukon par use penalty shootout ke liye majaboor hona padaa he
 On Thursday, he also had to decide the match against Russia through a penalty shootout, in which he won
 baharhaal, japan ke liye shiho shaakaai ne chauthe or akiko ota ne 31wein minute main gol kiye jabaki bharat ke liye saundarya yendalya ne 62wein or anupa barla ne 63wein minute main gol kiye
 India started badly and gave Japan a penalty corner in the third minute
 is par shiho ne koi galati nahin kii or ek lo-flik ke jariye apni team kaa khaataa khol diya
 After this, India tried vigorously for an equalizer
 bhartiya khilaadi prayatnsheel dikh rahi thim
 Many mistakes were also made in this sequence
 19wein minute main sushila chanu or 30wein minute main jasprit ko foul ke kaaran haraa card dikhaaya gaya
 In the 30th minute, Jasprit's mistake gave Japan another penalty corner, which Ota scored to put his team ahead 2–0
 madhyantar tak yahi score rahaa
 It was difficult for India but the Indian players did not lose courage and scored on the penalty corner in the 62nd minute to make it 1-2
 yah gol jasprit ke paas par saundarya ne kiya
 In the 63rd minute, India made another attack and managed to score an equalizer
 yah gol barla ne kiya
 Barla deflected Rani Rampal's hit to make the score 2-2
 nirdhaarit samay tak yahi score rahaa
 Now it was the penalty shootout
 bharat kii ore se sushila chanu pehle prayaas main gol nahin kar sakin jabaki japan kii ore se majuki arai ne gol kiya
 Japan was ahead 1-0
 bharat ke liye duusare prayaas main ritu rani naakaam raheen jabaki japan ke liye yuri nagai ne gol kiya
 Japan was ahead 2–0
 tippaniyan Vandana Kataria could not score a goal in the third attempt for India while Akiko Ota could not score for Japan as well
 score 2-0 hi rahaa
 Soundarya scored in the fourth attempt for India while Akiko Kato failed to score for Japan
 score 1-2 hi rahaa
 In the final attempt for India, Rani Rampal scored and the score was reduced to 2–2 but Rika Kamazawa from Japan gave her team the victory in the final attempt
 is toornament ke liye tay ex niyamon ke mutabik agar koi round robin match nirdhaarit samay tak barabari par rahata he to tiimon ko penalty shootout ke jariye nateeja nikaalnaa hota he
 The team that wins in a penalty shootout is called the winning draw (winning the draw) team, while the losing team is called the losing draw (losing team)
 drow jeetne vaali team ko do ank or haarane vaali team ko ek ank miltaa he
 Thus, India got one point from this match while Japan scored two
 japan ke ab 10 ank ho gaye hai
 India also has the same number of points, but due to the better performance of Japan in all the previous matches, India remains in the first place in the table of six teams
 japan duusare sthaan par he
 Japan have scored 25 goals against their opposition teams while India have scored 21 goals
 bharat ne teen match jite hai jabaki ek match main vah loojing drow team rahi he
 On the other hand, Japan has won two out of four matches while on two occasions it has been forced to a penalty shootout
 guuruuvaar ko rus ke khilaaf bhi use penalty shootout ke jariye match kaa faisla karnaa padaa tha, jisamen uski jeet hui thi
 Nonetheless, Shiho Shakai scored for Japan in the fourth and Akiko Ota scored in the 31st minute while for India Soundarya Yendalya scored 62nd and Anupa Barla scored in the 63rd minute
 bharat ne behad kharaab shuruyaat kii or tisare minute main hi japan ko penalty carnor de diya

 iske baad bharat ne barabari ke gol ke liye joardaar prayaas kiya

 is kram main unase kai galtiyaan bhi huin

 This was the score till midnight
